I thought I had turned the water on in the shower too much until I discovered it was water leaking from the ceiling, in front of the toilet. On the first day I checked in, I called the front desk and told them that there was no need for cleaning during my stay, and the door was always lit with Do Not Disturb, but there were still people who came in to clean without permission. I just asked whether there was any training. What's even worse is that the breakfast in the restaurant is getting worse day by day. I finally believe that the previous reviews are correct. On the morning of the third day of junior high school, there were pancakes, fruit pancakes and rice cakes, but they were all removed later on, so breakfast only consisted of disgusting bread and white glutinous rice. There was also one day where the ingredients beside the white glutinous rice were not available. They said that all the brown sugar was used last night and they went out to buy it now. What's even more amazing is the fat manager in their restaurant. While I was dining, he could spit a lot of phlegm in the lobby, making a loud and disgusting sound. There is a trash can next to their coffee machine, and there is also a place to put the audio controller, and there is also a trash can. During my meal, he took turns coughing and spitting it out. I was really convinced. Finally, I couldn't help but say it the day before. too disgusting. The biggest thing for him is to eat his bowl of beef noodles every day at work, and he has to eat it out of a takeout box. I get the seasonings and wait at the omelette stall, humming a little song while waiting for his omeletteüòìThe shop looks like Freshly squeezed apple juice is made by adding an apple to the beverage apple juice. I was thinking that everywhere else there was cucumber juice and carrot juice, so I was careless and drank an apple drink. Square dances and songs start from 7:30 every day until around 8:00 in the evening, and the executive rooms are not equipped with refrigerators.
